## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Connect REST API v1 to v2 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Connect REST API: the v1 connector resource handlers, the v2 connector resource handlers, and the version routing logic. Identify what changed between v1 and v2 in the task status and error response schemas.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

The `/workspace/answer.json` file has been created with my findings. Here's a summary:

## Kafka Connect REST API Analysis

### Resource Handler Files (all in `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489`)

| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java` | Main public connector resource handler (`@Path("/connectors")`) |
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/resources/InternalConnectResource.java` | Internal intra-cluster connector resource (extends `InternalClusterResource`) |
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/resources/InternalClusterResource.java` | Abstract base: task config PUT and zombie fencing endpoints |
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/resources/ConnectorPluginsResource.java` | Plugin discovery/validation |
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/resources/RootResource.java` | Root (`/`) with server info and health check |
| `connect/runtime/.../rest/ConnectRestServer.java` | Assembles and registers all resources (version routing) |

### Key Finding: No URL-based v1/v2 versioning
The codebase does **not** use `/v1/` or `/v2/` URL paths. The API evolution is captured in entity classes:

### Schema Changes (v1 → v2)

**Task/Connector Status (`ConnectorStateInfo.java`)**:
- v1: `id`, `state`, `worker_id`, `msg`
- v2: `id`, `state`, `worker_id`, **`trace`** (renamed from `msg`), **`version`** (added)
- Backward compat: constructors use `@JsonProperty("msg")` for deserialization, while the `trace()` getter serializes as `"trace"`

**Error Response (`ErrorMessage.java`)**:
- Unchanged across versions: `{"error_code": <int>, "message": <string>}`
- Produced by `ConnectExceptionMapper` from `ConnectRestException`
